    SELECT [a].[MergerName], [a].[ID], [a].[LevelType], [c].[ID] AS [ID0], [c].[Name], [c].[FullName], [c].[BusinessLicense], [c].[CorporationAddress], [c].[CreationTime], [c].[CreatorUserID], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[IsActive], [c].[LegalPersonIDCardNo], [c].[LastModificationTime], [c].[LegalPerson], [c].[LegalPersonPhone], [c].[FaxNumber], [c].[Remarks], [c].[SupportEMail], [c].[Telephone]
    FROM [Corporation] AS [c]
    LEFT JOIN [Area] AS [a] ON [c].[AreaID] = [a].[ID]
    WHERE [c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Department] AS [d] ON [t].[ID0] = [d].[CorporationID]
ORDER BY [t].[ID0], [d].[ID]
